***потребоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́боваться</a> (4201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребовать.html>потре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potrébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́боваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrébovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требоваться.html>тре́боваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to need, to require
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́буется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:программист.html>программи́ст</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam <b>potrébujetsja</b> programmíst.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We will <b>need</b> a programmer.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take (time, effort, money, etc. for something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́буется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na éto <b>potrébujetsja</b> mnógo vrémeni.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It will <b>take</b> a lot of time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***потрепать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a> (6204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrepátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull about, to blow about, to flutter, to tousle</li>
<li>to pat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>potrepátʹ</b> kovó-libo po plečú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pat smb's shoulder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to beat up, to maul, to pummel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосед.html>сосе́ди</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>во́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sosédi <b>potrepáli</b> vóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neighbours mauled the thief</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give a hard life/time
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žiznʹ <b>potrepála</b> jevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had a life full of trouble; his troubles had told on his appearance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mention too often, to make too many references <i>(to)</i>, to hackney
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne xóčetsja <b>potrepátʹ</b> éto vysókoje slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I wouldn't like to use this lofty word without a special reason</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сталь.html>ста́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вовсю.html>вовсю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pósle étoj istórii jevó ímja stáli <b>potrepátʹ</b> vovsjú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after that incident, his name became the talk of the town</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***потрошить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потрошить.html>потроши́ть</a> (22835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрошить.html>потроши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrošítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпотрошить.html>вы́потрошить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распотрошить.html>распотроши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disembowel, to eviscerate, to gut
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпотрошить.html>вы́потрошить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výpotrošitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to paunch

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потрясённый.html>потрясённый</a> (3178)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясённый.html>потрясённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrjasjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potrjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясённый.html>потрясённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrjasjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shocked, astonished, dumbfounded, speechless</li></ol>

***потрясать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потрясать.html>потряса́ть</a> (4850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potrjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясать.html>потряса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrjasátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shake, to brandish</li>
<li>to shake, to rock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основание.html>основа́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">potrjastí do osnovánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake to its foundation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясать.html>потряса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крик.html>кри́ками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>potrjasátʹ</b> vózdux kríkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rend the air with shouts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amaze, to astound, to shock, to astonish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потрясающий.html>потряса́юще</a> (17846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Adverbial form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясать.html>потряса́ющий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potrjasájuščij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">terrific, fabulous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясающий.html>потряса́юще</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrjasájušče</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stunningly, breathtakingly, amazingly, astonishingly</li>
<li>fantastically, sensationally, shockingly, strikingly</li>
<li>appallingly, horribly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трясти.html>трясти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trjastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потрясти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potrjastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясать.html>потряса́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потускнеть.html>потускне́ть</a> (14460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тускнеть.html>тускне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tusknétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потускнеть.html>потускне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">potusknétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тускнеть.html>тускне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow dim, to dull, to lose its lustre</li>
<li>to pale</li>
<li>to wane</li>
<li>to pale <i>(before)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторона́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">storoná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:потчевать.html>по́тчевать</a> (25007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">почьщивати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">počĭštivati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
